ANALYSIS   R-Matrix code SAMMY was used to analyze the total      1283700200009 
           cross section data to obtain resonance parameters.     1283700200010 
           Capture data were analyzed with Macklin's code         1283700200011 
            (ORNL-TM-4810)                                        1283700200012 
           . Spin values were determined from a                   1283700200013 
           detailed analysis of the magnitude and shape of the    1283700200014 
           transmission dip.                                      1283700200015 
           . Neutron widths were determined                       1283700200016 
           from transmission dip.                                 1283700200017 
           . G*Gamma-width is determined                          1283700200018 
           from G*neutron width and the capture area.             1283700200019 
CORRECTION Capture areas were corrected for resonance neutron     1283700200020 
           scattering into the gamma ray detectors. These         1283700200021 
           corrections were small in most cases.                  1283700200022 
ERR-ANALYS (DATA-ERR) No details given. Resonance neutron         1283700200023 
           energies (based on absolute neutron time of flight)    1283700200024 
           have about 0.08% accuracy.                             1283700200025 
FLAG       (1.) Spin 1/2- or 3/2-                                 1283700200026 
           (2.) Seen only in capture data.The G*Gamma-width       1283700200027 
           represents the G*neutron width since the gamma         1283700200028 
           width is about 0.3 eV.                                 1283700200029 
           (3.) Spin value doubtful.                              1283700200030 
           (4.)A p1/2 contribution in addition to an s-wave       1283700200031 
           resonance was required to fit the transmission         1283700200032 
           dip near 270 keV.                                      1283700200033
